import pandas as pd from datetime import

datetime, timedelta import json class TimeTracker: def __init__(self,

sheet_key, credentials_path): # Google

# æ¥­å‹™ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªå®šç¾© self.categories =

{ 'ä¼šè­°': {'è‡ªå‹•åŒ–å¯èƒ½': True, 'ROIå„ªå…ˆåº¦': 4}, 'ãƒ¬ãƒãƒ¼ãƒˆä½œæˆ': {'è‡ªå‹•åŒ–å¯èƒ½':

log_activity(self, category, duration, description=""): """æ´»å‹•ã‚’è¨˜éŒ²"""

worksheet =

def analyze_weekly_data(self): """é€±æ¬¡åˆ†æã‚’å®Ÿè¡Œ""" worksheet =

self.sheet.worksheet('æ™‚é–“ãƒ­ã‚°') records =

week_ago] # ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªåˆ¥é›†è¨ˆ category_summary = weekly_data.groupby('ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒª')

['æ™‚é–“(åˆ†)'].sum() #

è‡ªå‹•åŒ–å¯èƒ½æ¥­å‹™ã®ç‰¹å®š automatable = weekly_data[weekly_data['è‡ªå‹•åŒ–å¯èƒ½'] ==

True] automation_potential =

automatable.groupby('ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒª')['æ™‚é–“(åˆ†)'].sum() # ROIè¨ˆç®— hourly_rate =

5000 # æ™‚çµ¦ï¼ˆå††ï¼‰

hourly_rate annual_saving = weekly_cost_saving * 52 return { 'ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªåˆ¥æ™‚

é–“': category_summary.to_dict(),

'è‡ªå‹•åŒ–å¯èƒ½æ™‚é–“': automation_potential.to_dict(), 'é€±æ¬¡å‰Šæ¸›å¯èƒ½é¡':

= self.analyze_weekly_data() report

= f""" ğŸ“Š é€±æ¬¡æ™‚é–“åˆ†æãƒ¬ãƒãƒ¼ãƒˆ ç”Ÿæˆæ—¥æ™‚: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d

%H:%M:%S')} ã€ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªåˆ¥æ™‚é–“é…åˆ†ã€‘

""" for category, minutes in analysis['ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªåˆ¥æ™‚é–“'].items(): hours =

{hours:.1f}æ™‚é–“ ({percentage:.1f}%)\n"

åŒ–å¯èƒ½æ™‚é–“'].values()) /

{analysis['å¹´é–“å‰Šæ¸›å¯èƒ½é¡']:,.0f}å†† ã€æ¨å¥¨è‡ªå‹•åŒ–é †ä½ã€‘ """ # ROIé †ã§ã‚½ãƒ¼ãƒˆ

å„ªå…ˆåº¦'], reverse=True ) for i,

self.categories[category]['ROIå„ªå…ˆåº¦'] report += f" {i}ä½: {category}

({minutes/60:.1f}æ™‚é–“/é€±, ROI: {'â˜…' *

roi_score})\n" return report # ä½¿ç”¨ä¾‹ if __name__ == "__main__": # åˆæœŸåŒ–

åˆ†æãƒ¬ãƒãƒ¼ãƒˆç”Ÿæˆ report =

## ãƒšãƒ¼ã‚¸ 9

fetch_project_progress(self) -> Dict: """Jiraã‹ã‚‰ãƒ—ãƒ­ã‚¸ã‚§ã‚¯ãƒˆé€²æ—ã‚’å–å¾—"""

calculate_avg_review_time(self, prs: List) ->

float: """å¹³å‡ãƒ¬ãƒ“ãƒ¥ãƒ¼æ™‚é–“ã‚’è¨ˆç®—""" review_times = [] for pr in prs: if

pr['merged_at'] and pr['created_at']:

created = datetime.fromisoformat(pr['created_at'].replace('Z', '+00:00'))

datetime.fromisoformat(pr['merged_at'].replace('Z', '+00:00'))

created).total_seconds() / 3600) # æ™‚é–“å˜ä½ return sum(review_times) /

len(review_times) if review_times else 0

# ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’çµ±åˆ for project in

pd.DataFrame(projects_data) def _fetch_jira_projects(self) -> List[Dict]:

"""Jiraã‹ã‚‰å®Œäº†æ¸ˆã¿ãƒ—ãƒ­ã‚¸ã‚§ã‚¯ãƒˆæƒ…å ±ã‚’å–å¾—""" headers = { 'Authorization':

å»1å¹´ã®å®Œäº†ãƒ—ãƒ­ã‚¸ã‚§ã‚¯ãƒˆã‚’å–å¾— jql =

"project = MAIN AND status = Done AND updated >= -52w" url =

f"{self.api_configs['jira']['base_url']}/rest/api/3/search" response =

params={'jql': jql, 'maxResults': 100}) if response.status_code == 200:

issues = response.json()['issues']

projects = [] for issue in issues: fields = issue['fields'] # æœŸé–“è¨ˆç®—

created =

datetime.fromisoformat(fields['created'].replace('Z', '+00:00')) resolved

=

datetime.fromisoformat(fields['resolutiondate'].replace('Z', '+00:00'))

created).days project = { 'id': issue['key'], 'planned_duration':

_calculate_complexity_score(self, fields: Dict) -> float: """ãƒ—ãƒ­ã‚¸ã‚§ã‚¯ãƒˆã®

è¤‡é›‘åº¦ã‚¹ã‚³ã‚¢ã‚’è¨ˆç®—""" score = 0.0 #

å„ªå…ˆåº¦ã«ã‚ˆã‚‹åŠ ç®— priority = fields.get('priority', {}).get('name', 'Medium')

priority_scores = {'Highest': 1.0,

'High': 0.8, 'Medium': 0.5, 'Low': 0.2} score +=

priority_scores.get(priority, 0.5) # ã‚³ãƒ³ãƒãƒ¼ãƒãƒ³ãƒˆæ•°ã«ã‚ˆã‚‹åŠ ç®—

components = fields.get('components', []) score += len(components) * 0.1 #

èª¬æ˜æ–‡ã®é•·ã•ã«ã‚ˆã‚‹åŠ ç®—ï¼ˆè¤‡é›‘ãªè¦æ±‚ã»ã©é•·æ–‡ï¼‰ description_length =

len(fields.get('description', '')) score +=

min(description_length / 1000, 0.5) return min(score, 2.0) # æœ€å¤§2.0 def

## ãƒšãƒ¼ã‚¸ 31

pd.DataFrame) -> Dict: """æ©Ÿæ¢°å­¦ç¿’ãƒ¢ãƒ‡ãƒ«ã‚’è¨“ç·´""" X =

StandardScaler() X_scaled = scaler.fit_transform(X)

self.scalers['features'] = scaler results = {} #

é…å»¶äºˆæ¸¬ãƒ¢ãƒ‡ãƒ« y_delay = df['is_delayed'] X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test =

(delay_predictions == y_test).mean() self.models['delay_classifier'] =

delay_model # ã‚³ã‚¹ãƒˆè¶…éäºˆæ¸¬ãƒ¢ãƒ‡ãƒ« y_cost

= df['cost_overrun_ratio'] X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test =

self.models['cost_regressor'] = cost_model #

å“è³ªå•é¡Œäºˆæ¸¬ãƒ¢ãƒ‡ãƒ« y_quality = df['quality_issues'] X_train, X_test, y_train,

results def predict_project_risks(self,

project_data: Dict) -> Dict: """ç¾åœ¨ã®ãƒ—ãƒ­ã‚¸ã‚§ã‚¯ãƒˆã®ãƒªã‚¹ã‚¯ã‚’äºˆæ¸¬""" # ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’ç‰¹

å¾´é‡å½¢å¼ã«å¤‰æ› feature_dict =

self.models['delay_classifier'].predict_proba(X_scaled)[0][1] cost_ratio =

self.models['cost_regressor'].predict(X_scaled)[0] quality_prob =

self.models['quality_classifier'].predict_proba(X_scaled)[0][1] # ç·åˆãƒªã‚¹

ã‚¯ã‚¹ã‚³ã‚¢ overall_risk = (delay_prob *

0.4 + max(cost_ratio - 1, 0) * 0.3 + quality_prob * 0.3) return {

'overall_risk_score': min(overall_risk, 1.0),

'delay_probability': delay_prob, 'cost_overrun_ratio': cost_ratio,

'quality_risk_probability': quality_prob,

'risk_level': self._categorize_risk(overall_risk), 'recommendations':

self._generate_recommendations(delay_prob,

cost_ratio, quality_prob) } def _categorize_risk(self, risk_score: float)

-> str: """ãƒªã‚¹ã‚¯ã‚¹ã‚³ã‚¢ã‚’ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªåŒ–"""

if risk_score >= 0.7: return "ğŸ”´ é«˜ãƒªã‚¹ã‚¯" elif risk_score >= 0.4: return

"ğŸŸ¡ ä¸­ãƒªã‚¹ã‚¯" else: return "ğŸŸ¢

ä½ãƒªã‚¹ã‚¯" def _generate_recommendations(self, delay_prob: float,

List[str]: """ãƒªã‚¹ã‚¯è¦å› ã«åŸºã¥ãæ¨å¥¨ã‚¢ã‚¯ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³""" recommendations = [] if

ãƒªã‚½ãƒ¼ã‚¹è¿½åŠ ï¼šãƒãƒ¼ãƒ å¢—å“¡ã¾ãŸã¯ã‚¹ã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ—å‰Šæ¸›") if cost_ratio > 1.3:

ã‚³ã‚¹ãƒˆç®¡ç†å¼·åŒ–ï¼šäºˆç®—ã®è©³ç´°ãƒ¢ãƒ‹ã‚¿ãƒªãƒ³ã‚°é–‹å§‹") recommendations.append("ğŸ” åŠ¹ç‡æ€§æ”¹

åŒ–") recommendations.append("ğŸ“‹

ãƒ¬ãƒ“ãƒ¥ãƒ¼é »åº¦å¢—åŠ ï¼šã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ãƒ¬ãƒ“ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ã®å¾¹åº•") return recommendations def

import pandas as pd

import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

import matplotlib.dates as mdates

from datetime import datetime, timedelta

from reportlab.lib.pagesizes import A4

from reportlab.lib import colors

from reportlab.lib.styles import getSampleStyleSheet, ParagraphStyle

from reportlab.platypus import SimpleDocTemplate, Paragraph, Spacer, Table,

TableStyle, Image, PageBreak

from reportlab.lib.units import cm

import requests

import json

from typing import Dict, List

import io

class OneOnOnePrepSystem:

def __init__(self, api_configs: Dict):

---

## ãƒšãƒ¼ã‚¸ 40

"""1on1æº–å‚™ã‚·ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒ ã‚’åˆæœŸåŒ–"""

self.api_configs = api_configs

self.styles = getSampleStyleSheet()

def collect_member_data(self, member_id: str, weeks_back: int = 2) -> Dict:

"""ãƒ¡ãƒ³ãƒãƒ¼ã®æ´»å‹•ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’åé›†"""

end_date = datetime.now()

start_date = end_date - timedelta(weeks=weeks_back)

data = {

'member_id': member_id,

'period': f"{start_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')} ~

{end_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}",

'github_stats': self._fetch_github_stats(member_id, start_date,

end_date),

'jira_stats': self._fetch_jira_stats(member_id, start_date, end_date),

'slack_stats': self._fetch_slack_stats(member_id, start_date,

end_date),

'calendar_stats': self._fetch_calendar_stats(member_id, start_date,

end_date),

'previous_followup': self._fetch_previous_followup(member_id)

}

return data

def _fetch_github_stats(self, member_id: str, start_date: datetime, end_date:

datetime) -> Dict:

"""GitHubã‹ã‚‰é–‹ç™ºçµ±è¨ˆã‚’å–å¾—"""

# GitHub APIèªè¨¼

headers = {

'Authorization': f"token {self.api_configs['github']['token']}",

'Accept': 'application/vnd.github.v3+json'

}

# ãƒªãƒã‚¸ãƒˆãƒªå–å¾—

repo = self.api_configs['github']['repo']

# ã‚³ãƒŸãƒƒãƒˆæ•°å–å¾—

commits_url = f"https://api.github.com/repos/{repo}/commits"

commits = requests.get(

commits_url,

headers=headers,

params={

'author': member_id,

'since': start_date.isoformat(),

'until': end_date.isoformat()

}

).json()

# ãƒ—ãƒ«ãƒªã‚¯ã‚¨ã‚¹ãƒˆæ•°å–å¾—

prs_url = f"https://api.github.com/repos/{repo}/pulls"

prs = requests.get(

prs_url,

headers=headers,

params={

'creator': member_id,

'state': 'all',

'since': start_date.isoformat()

}

).json()

# ãƒ¬ãƒ“ãƒ¥ãƒ¼å‚åŠ æ•°

reviews_count = 0

for pr in prs:

reviews_url = pr.get('url', '') + '/reviews'

reviews = requests.get(reviews_url, headers=headers).json()

reviews_count += len(reviews) if isinstance(reviews, list) else 0

return {

'commits': len(commits) if isinstance(commits, list) else 0,

'pull_requests': len(prs) if isinstance(prs, list) else 0,

'code_reviews': reviews_count,

'avg_commits_per_day': len(commits) / 14 if isinstance(commits, list)

else 0

}

def _fetch_jira_stats(self, member_id: str, start_date: datetime, end_date:

datetime) -> Dict:

"""Jiraã‹ã‚‰ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯çµ±è¨ˆã‚’å–å¾—"""

headers = {

'Authorization': f"Bearer {self.api_configs['jira']['token']}",

'Accept': 'application/json'

}

# å®Œäº†ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯

jql_completed = f"assignee = {member_id} AND status = Done AND resolved >=

---

## ãƒšãƒ¼ã‚¸ 41

{start_date.strftime('%Y-%m-%d')}"

completed_url = f"{self.api_configs['jira']

['base_url']}/rest/api/3/search"

completed = requests.get(completed_url, headers=headers, params={'jql':

jql_completed}).json()

# é€²è¡Œä¸­ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯

jql_in_progress = f"assignee = {member_id} AND status = 'In Progress'"

in_progress = requests.get(completed_url, headers=headers, params={'jql':

jql_in_progress}).json()

# æœŸé™è¶…éã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯

jql_overdue = f"assignee = {member_id} AND status != Done AND duedate <

now()"

overdue = requests.get(completed_url, headers=headers, params={'jql':

jql_overdue}).json()

return {

'completed_tasks': completed.get('total', 0),

'in_progress_tasks': in_progress.get('total', 0),

'overdue_tasks': overdue.get('total', 0),

'completion_rate':

self._calculate_completion_rate(completed.get('issues', []))

}

def _calculate_completion_rate(self, issues: List) -> float:

"""ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯å®Œäº†ç‡ã‚’è¨ˆç®—ï¼ˆäºˆå®šæ™‚é–“ã«å¯¾ã™ã‚‹å®Ÿç¸¾ï¼‰"""

if not issues:

return 100.0

total_estimated = 0

total_actual = 0

for issue in issues:

estimated = issue['fields'].get('timeoriginalestimate', 0)

actual = issue['fields'].get('timespent', 0)

if estimated > 0:

total_estimated += estimated

total_actual += actual

if total_estimated == 0:

return 100.0

return min((total_estimated / total_actual) * 100, 200.0) if total_actual

> 0 else 0.0

def _fetch_slack_stats(self, member_id: str, start_date: datetime, end_date:

datetime) -> Dict:

"""Slackã‹ã‚‰ã‚³ãƒŸãƒ¥ãƒ‹ã‚±ãƒ¼ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³çµ±è¨ˆã‚’å–å¾—"""

headers = {

'Authorization': f"Bearer {self.api_configs['slack']['token']}"

}

# ãƒ¡ãƒƒã‚»ãƒ¼ã‚¸æ•°ï¼ˆç°¡ç•¥åŒ–ï¼šå®Ÿéš›ã¯conversations.historyã‚’ä½¿ç”¨ï¼‰

return {

'messages_sent': 120, # ãƒ€ãƒŸãƒ¼ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿

'channels_active': 8,

'avg_response_time_hours': 1.5,

'emoji_reactions': 45

}

def _fetch_calendar_stats(self, member_id: str, start_date: datetime,

end_date: datetime) -> Dict:

"""ã‚«ãƒ¬ãƒ³ãƒ€ãƒ¼ã‹ã‚‰ä¼šè­°çµ±è¨ˆã‚’å–å¾—"""

# Google Calendar APIï¼ˆç°¡ç•¥åŒ–ï¼‰

return {

'total_meetings': 12,

'meeting_hours': 18.5,

'focus_time_hours': 25.5,

'work_hours_total': 44.0

}

"""å‰å›1on1ã®ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚¢ãƒƒãƒ—é …ç›®ã‚’å–å¾—"""

# ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹ã¾ãŸã¯ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã‹ã‚‰å–å¾—ï¼ˆç°¡ç•¥åŒ–ï¼‰

'status': 'é”æˆ',

## ãƒšãƒ¼ã‚¸ 42

'deadline': '2024-02-01'

]

def analyze_performance(self, data: Dict) -> Dict:

"""ãƒ‘ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒãƒ³ã‚¹åˆ†æã¨ç•°å¸¸æ¤œå‡º"""

github = data['github_stats']

jira = data['jira_stats']

calendar = data['calendar_stats']

analysis = {

'health_score': 0.0,

'alerts': [],

'strengths': [],

'concerns': []

}

# å¥åº·ã‚¹ã‚³ã‚¢è¨ˆç®—ï¼ˆ0-100ï¼‰

score = 70 # ãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹

# ç”Ÿç”£æ€§æŒ‡æ¨™

if github['avg_commits_per_day'] >= 2:

score += 10

analysis['strengths'].append('âœ… ã‚³ãƒŸãƒƒãƒˆé »åº¦ãŒé«˜ãã€é–‹ç™ºãŒé †èª¿')

elif github['avg_commits_per_day'] < 0.5:

score -= 15

analysis['concerns'].append('âš  ã‚³ãƒŸãƒƒãƒˆæ•°ãŒå°‘ãªã„ï¼ˆå¹³å‡0.5/æ—¥æœªæº€ï¼‰')

analysis['alerts'].append('ç”Ÿç”£æ€§ä½ä¸‹ã®å¯èƒ½æ€§ã€‚ãƒ–ãƒ­ãƒƒã‚«ãƒ¼ãŒãªã„ã‹ç¢ºèª')

# ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯å®Œäº†çŠ¶æ³

if jira['completion_rate'] >= 90:

score += 10

analysis['strengths'].append('âœ… ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯å®Œäº†ç‡ãŒé«˜ã„ï¼ˆ90%ä»¥ä¸Šï¼‰')

elif jira['completion_rate'] < 70:

score -= 10

analysis['concerns'].append('âš  ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯å®Œäº†ç‡ãŒä½ã„ï¼ˆ70%æœªæº€ï¼‰')

# æœŸé™è¶…é

if jira['overdue_tasks'] > 3:

score -= 15

analysis['alerts'].append('ğŸš¨ æœŸé™è¶…éã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯ãŒå¤šã„ï¼ˆ3ä»¶ä»¥ä¸Šï¼‰ã€‚å„ªå…ˆé †ä½ã®è¦‹ç›´

ã—ãŒå¿…è¦')

# ä¼šè­°éå¤šãƒã‚§ãƒƒã‚¯

meeting_ratio = calendar['meeting_hours'] / calendar['work_hours_total']

if meeting_ratio > 0.5:

score -= 10

analysis['alerts'].append('ğŸš¨ ä¼šè­°æ™‚é–“ãŒéå¤šï¼ˆ50%è¶…ï¼‰ã€‚é›†ä¸­æ™‚é–“ã®ç¢ºä¿ãŒå¿…

è¦')

# ã‚³ãƒ©ãƒœãƒ¬ãƒ¼ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³

if github['code_reviews'] >= 5:

score += 5

analysis['strengths'].append('âœ… ã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ãƒ¬ãƒ“ãƒ¥ãƒ¼ã«ç©æ¥µçš„')

analysis['health_score'] = max(0, min(100, score))

return analysis

def generate_discussion_topics(self, data: Dict, analysis: Dict) ->

List[Dict]:

"""è­°é¡Œã‚’è‡ªå‹•ç”Ÿæˆ"""

topics = []

# ã‚¢ãƒ©ãƒ¼ãƒˆãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹ã®è­°é¡Œ

for alert in analysis['alerts']:

topics.append({

'ä½•ãŒãƒ–ãƒ­ãƒƒã‚«ãƒ¼ã«ãªã£ã¦ã„ã¾ã™ã‹ï¼Ÿ',

'ã‚µãƒãƒ¼ãƒˆã§ãã‚‹ã“ã¨ã¯ã‚ã‚Šã¾ã™ã‹ï¼Ÿ',

'å„ªå…ˆé †ä½ã‚’è¦‹ç›´ã™å¿…è¦ãŒã‚ã‚Šã¾ã™ã‹ï¼Ÿ'

]

})

# ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚¢ãƒƒãƒ—è­°é¡Œ

for followup in data['previous_followup']:

if followup['status'] == 'é€²è¡Œä¸­':

topics.append({

'priority': 'ä¸­',

'category': 'ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚¢ãƒƒãƒ—',

'topic': f"å‰å›ã®ç´„æŸï¼š{followup['item']}",

'suggested_questions': [

f"é€²æ—ï¼š{followup['progress']}",

---

## ãƒšãƒ¼ã‚¸ 43

'è¨ˆç”»é€šã‚Šé€²ã‚“ã§ã„ã¾ã™ã‹ï¼Ÿ',

'è¿½åŠ ã®ã‚µãƒãƒ¼ãƒˆãŒå¿…è¦ã§ã™ã‹ï¼Ÿ'

]

})

# æˆé•·ãƒ»ã‚­ãƒ£ãƒªã‚¢

topics.append({

'priority': 'ä¸­',

'category': 'æˆé•·ãƒ»ã‚­ãƒ£ãƒªã‚¢',

'topic': 'ã‚¹ã‚­ãƒ«é–‹ç™ºã¨ä»Šå¾Œã®ã‚­ãƒ£ãƒªã‚¢',

return sorted(topics, key=lambda x: {'é«˜': 1, 'ä¸­': 2, 'ä½': 3}

def create_visualization(self, data: Dict) -> str:

"""ã‚°ãƒ©ãƒ•ã‚’ç”Ÿæˆã—ã¦ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ãƒ‘ã‚¹ã‚’è¿”ã™"""

fig, axes = plt.subplots(2, 2, figsize=(12, 10))

fig.suptitle('ãƒ¡ãƒ³ãƒãƒ¼æ´»å‹•ã‚µãƒãƒªãƒ¼', fontsize=16, fontweight='bold')

# ã‚°ãƒ©ãƒ•1ï¼šGitHubæ´»å‹•

ax1 = axes[0, 0]

github = data['github_stats']

categories = ['Commits', 'Pull Requests', 'Code Reviews']

values = [github['commits'], github['pull_requests'],

github['code_reviews']]

ax1.bar(categories, values, color=['#4CAF50', '#2196F3', '#FF9800'])

ax1.set_title('GitHub Activity')

ax1.set_ylabel('Count')

# ã‚°ãƒ©ãƒ•2ï¼šJiraã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯çŠ¶æ³

ax2 = axes[0, 1]

jira = data['jira_stats']

labels = ['Completed', 'In Progress', 'Overdue']

sizes = [jira['completed_tasks'], jira['in_progress_tasks'],

jira['overdue_tasks']]

colors_pie = ['#4CAF50', '#FFC107', '#F44336']

ax2.pie(sizes, labels=labels, colors=colors_pie, autopct='%1.0f%%',

startangle=90)

ax2.set_title('Task Distribution')

# ã‚°ãƒ©ãƒ•3ï¼šæ™‚é–“é…åˆ†

ax3 = axes[1, 0]

calendar = data['calendar_stats']

time_labels = ['Meeting', 'Focus Time', 'Other']

time_values = [

calendar['meeting_hours'],

calendar['focus_time_hours'],

calendar['work_hours_total'] - calendar['meeting_hours'] -

calendar['focus_time_hours']

]

ax3.barh(time_labels, time_values, color=['#E91E63', '#9C27B0',

'#607D8B'])

ax3.set_title('Time Allocation (hours)')

ax3.set_xlabel('Hours')

# ã‚°ãƒ©ãƒ•4ï¼šå®Œäº†ç‡ãƒˆãƒ¬ãƒ³ãƒ‰ï¼ˆãƒ€ãƒŸãƒ¼ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ï¼‰

ax4 = axes[1, 1]

weeks = ['Week 1', 'Week 2', 'Week 3', 'Week 4']

completion_trend = [85, 78, 92, jira['completion_rate']]

ax4.plot(weeks, completion_trend, marker='o', linewidth=2, markersize=8,

color='#3F51B5')

ax4.axhline(y=80, color='r', linestyle='--', label='Target (80%)')

ax4.set_title('Task Completion Rate Trend')

ax4.set_ylabel('Completion Rate (%)')

ax4.legend()

ax4.set_ylim(0, 100)

plt.tight_layout()

---

## ãƒšãƒ¼ã‚¸ 44

# ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã«ä¿å­˜

filepath =

f'/tmp/1on1_report_{data["member_id"]}_{datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d")}.png'

plt.savefig(filepath, dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')

plt.close()

return filepath

def generate_pdf_report(self, member_name: str, data: Dict, analysis: Dict,

topics: List[Dict], chart_path: str) -> str:

"""PDFè³‡æ–™ã‚’ç”Ÿæˆ"""

filename =

f'1on1_prep_{member_name}_{datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d")}.pdf'

doc = SimpleDocTemplate(filename, pagesize=A4)

story = []

# ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«

title_style = ParagraphStyle(

'CustomTitle',

parent=self.styles['Heading1'],

fontSize=24,

textColor=colors.HexColor('#1976D2'),

spaceAfter=30,

alignment=1 # Center

)

story.append(Paragraph(f'1on1æº–å‚™è³‡æ–™ï¼š{member_name}', title_style))

story.append(Paragraph(f'æœŸé–“ï¼š{data["period"]}', self.styles['Normal']))

story.append(Spacer(1, 1*cm))

# å¥åº·ã‚¹ã‚³ã‚¢

score = analysis['health_score']

score_color = colors.green if score >= 80 else colors.orange if score >=

60 else colors.red

score_style = ParagraphStyle('Score', parent=self.styles['Heading2'],

textColor=score_color)

story.append(Paragraph(f'å¥åº·ã‚¹ã‚³ã‚¢: {score:.0f}/100', score_style))

story.append(Spacer(1, 0.5*cm))

# ã‚¢ãƒ©ãƒ¼ãƒˆ

if analysis['alerts']:

story.append(Paragraph('ğŸš¨ é‡è¦ãªã‚¢ãƒ©ãƒ¼ãƒˆ', self.styles['Heading3']))

for alert in analysis['alerts']:

story.append(Paragraph(f'â€¢ {alert}', self.styles['Normal']))

story.append(Spacer(1, 0.5*cm))

# å¼·ã¿

if analysis['strengths']:

story.append(Paragraph('âœ… å¼·ã¿ãƒ»è‰¯ã„ç‚¹', self.styles['Heading3']))

for strength in analysis['strengths']:

story.append(Paragraph(f'â€¢ {strength}', self.styles['Normal']))

story.append(Spacer(1, 0.5*cm))

# ã‚°ãƒ©ãƒ•æŒ¿å…¥

story.append(PageBreak())

story.append(Paragraph('ğŸ“Š æ´»å‹•ã‚µãƒãƒªãƒ¼', self.styles['Heading2']))

story.append(Spacer(1, 0.5*cm))

story.append(Image(chart_path, width=18*cm, height=15*cm))

# å‰å›ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚¢ãƒƒãƒ—

story.append(PageBreak())

story.append(Paragraph('ğŸ“ å‰å›1on1ã®ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ­ãƒ¼ã‚¢ãƒƒãƒ—',

self.styles['Heading2']))

story.append(Spacer(1, 0.5*cm))

followup_data = [['é …ç›®', 'ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚¹', 'é€²æ—', 'æœŸé™']]

for item in data['previous_followup']:

followup_data.append([

item['item'],

item['status'],

item['progress'],

item['deadline']

])

followup_table = Table(followup_data, colWidths=[6*cm, 2.5*cm, 5*cm,

2.5*cm])

followup_table.setStyle(TableStyle([

('BACKGROUND', (0, 0), (-1, 0), colors.grey),

('TEXTCOLOR', (0, 0), (-1, 0), colors.whitesmoke),

('ALIGN', (0, 0), (-1, -1), 'LEFT'),

('FONTNAME', (0, 0), (-1, 0), 'Helvetica-Bold'),

('FONTSIZE', (0, 0), (-1, 0), 12),

('BOTTOMPADDING', (0, 0), (-1, 0), 12),

('BACKGROUND', (0, 1), (-1, -1), colors.beige),

('GRID', (0, 0), (-1, -1), 1, colors.black)

]))

---

## ãƒšãƒ¼ã‚¸ 45

story.append(followup_table)

# è­°é¡Œææ¡ˆ

story.append(PageBreak())

story.append(Paragraph('ğŸ’¡ ä»Šå›ã®è­°é¡Œï¼ˆå„ªå…ˆåº¦é †ï¼‰', self.styles['Heading2']))

story.append(Spacer(1, 0.5*cm))

for i, topic in enumerate(topics[:5]): # ä¸Šä½5ã¤

priority_colors = {'é«˜': colors.red, 'ä¸­': colors.orange, 'ä½':

colors.green}

topic_style = ParagraphStyle(

f'Topic{i}',

parent=self.styles['Heading3'],

textColor=priority_colors[topic['priority']]

)

story.append(Paragraph(f"{i+1}. [{topic['priority']}]

{topic['topic']}", topic_style))

story.append(Paragraph(f"ã‚«ãƒ†ã‚´ãƒªï¼š{topic['category']}",

self.styles['Normal']))

story.append(Paragraph('è³ªå•ä¾‹ï¼š', self.styles['Normal']))

for question in topic['suggested_questions']:

story.append(Paragraph(f' â€¢ {question}', self.styles['Normal']))

story.append(Spacer(1, 0.5*cm))

# PDFç”Ÿæˆ

doc.build(story)

return filename

def prepare_one_on_one(self, member_id: str, member_name: str) -> str:

"""1on1æº–å‚™ã®å®Œå…¨ãƒ•ãƒ­ãƒ¼"""

print(f"ğŸ“Š {member_name}ã®ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’åé›†ä¸­...")

data = self.collect_member_data(member_id)

print("ğŸ§  ãƒ‘ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒãƒ³ã‚¹ã‚’åˆ†æä¸­...")

analysis = self.analyze_performance(data)

print("ğŸ’¡ è­°é¡Œã‚’ç”Ÿæˆä¸­...")

topics = self.generate_discussion_topics(data, analysis)

print("ğŸ“ˆ ã‚°ãƒ©ãƒ•ã‚’ç”Ÿæˆä¸­...")

chart_path = self.create_visualization(data)

print("ğŸ“„ PDFè³‡æ–™ã‚’ä½œæˆä¸­...")

pdf_path = self.generate_pdf_report(member_name, data, analysis, topics,

chart_path)

print(f"âœ… å®Œæˆï¼ {pdf_path}")

return pdf_path

# ä½¿ç”¨ä¾‹

if __name__ == "__main__":

api_configs = {

'github': {

'token': 'your_github_token',

'repo': 'your-org/your-repo'

},

'jira': {

'token': 'your_jira_token',

'base_url': 'https://your-domain.atlassian.net'

},

'slack': {

'token': 'your_slack_token'

}

}

prep_system = OneOnOnePrepSystem(api_configs)

# 1on1æº–å‚™ã‚’å®Ÿè¡Œ

pdf_path = prep_system.prepare_one_on_one(

member_id='tanaka_taro',

member_name='ç”°ä¸­å¤ªéƒ'

)

print(f"\nğŸ¯ æº–å‚™å®Œäº†ï¼è³‡æ–™ï¼š{pdf_path}")

print("ğŸ“§ ãƒ¡ãƒ³ãƒãƒ¼ã«äº‹å‰å…±æœ‰ã—ã¦ã€å½“æ—¥ã¯å¯¾è©±ã«é›†ä¸­ã—ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†")

5. å®Ÿè£…æ‰‹é †ï¼ˆ3ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒƒãƒ—ï¼‰

## ãƒšãƒ¼ã‚¸ 46

ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒƒãƒ—1ï¼šç’°å¢ƒæº–å‚™ï¼ˆ5åˆ†ï¼‰

ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒƒãƒ—2ï¼šåˆå›å®Ÿè¡Œï¼ˆ5åˆ†ï¼‰

ãƒ¡ãƒ³ãƒãƒ¼IDã¨APIè¨­å®šã‚’å…¥åŠ›

python one_on_one_prep.py ã§è³‡æ–™ç”Ÿæˆ

ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒƒãƒ—3ï¼šè‡ªå‹•åŒ–è¨­å®šï¼ˆ2åˆ†ï¼‰

## ãƒšãƒ¼ã‚¸ 55

import os import subprocess from openai import OpenAI from datetime import

datetime import json import requests

from typing import Dict, List class MeetingTranscriber: def __init__(self,

openai_key: str, slack_webhook: str =

None): """è­°äº‹éŒ²è‡ªå‹•ç”Ÿæˆã‚·ã‚¹ãƒ†ãƒ ã‚’åˆæœŸåŒ–""" self.client =

OpenAI(api_key=openai_key) self.slack_webhook =

slack_webhook def extract_audio_from_video(self, video_path: str) -> str:

"""å‹•ç”»ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã‹ã‚‰éŸ³å£°ã‚’æŠ½å‡º"""

audio_path = video_path.replace('.mp4', '_audio.wav') # ffmpegã§éŸ³å£°æŠ½å‡º

command = [ 'ffmpeg', '-i', video_path,

'-vn', # å‹•ç”»ã‚¹ãƒˆãƒªãƒ¼ãƒ ç„¡åŠ¹ '-acodec', 'pcm_s16le', # 16bit PCM '-ar',

'16000', # 16kHz '-ac', '1', # ãƒ¢ãƒãƒ©ãƒ«

audio_path, '-y' # ä¸Šæ›¸ã ] try: subprocess.run(command, check=True,

capture_output=True) print(f"âœ…

éŸ³å£°æŠ½å‡ºå®Œäº†: {audio_path}") return audio_path except

subprocess.CalledProcessError as e: print(f"âŒ

éŸ³å£°æŠ½å‡ºã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼: {e}") return None def transcribe_audio(self, audio_path:

str) -> str: """Whisper

APIã§éŸ³å£°ã‚’ãƒ†ã‚­ã‚¹ãƒˆåŒ–""" try: with open(audio_path, 'rb') as audio_file:

self.client.audio.transcriptions.create( model="whisper-1",

file=audio_file, response_format="text",

language="ja" # æ—¥æœ¬èªæŒ‡å®š ) print(f"âœ… éŸ³å£°èªè­˜å®Œäº†: {len(transcript)}æ–‡å­—")

return transcript except Exception

as e: print(f"âŒ éŸ³å£°èªè­˜ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼: {e}") return None def

structure_minutes(self, transcript: str, meeting_title:

str = "") -> Dict: """GPT-4ã§è­°äº‹éŒ²ã‚’æ§‹é€ åŒ–""" structuring_prompt = f"""

ä»¥ä¸‹ã®ä¼šè­°ã®éŸ³å£°èªè­˜çµæœã‹ã‚‰ã€æ§‹é€ åŒ–ã•ã‚ŒãŸè­°äº‹éŒ²ã‚’ç”Ÿæˆã—ã¦ãã ã•ã„ã€‚ ã€ä¼šè­°ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«ã€‘

{meeting_title or "ä¼šè­°"}

ã€éŸ³å£°èªè­˜çµæœã€‘ {transcript} ä»¥ä¸‹ã®JSONå½¢å¼ã§å‡ºåŠ›ã—ã¦ãã ã•ã„ï¼š {{

"meeting_title": "ä¼šè­°ã®ã‚¿ã‚¤ãƒˆãƒ«", "date":

"YYYY-MM-DD", "participants": ["å‚åŠ è€…1", "å‚åŠ è€…2"], "agenda_items": [ {{

"topic": "è­°é¡Œ", "discussion":

"è­°è«–å†…å®¹ã®è¦ç´„", "decisions": ["æ±ºå®šäº‹é …1", "æ±ºå®šäº‹é …2"], "action_items": [ {{

"task": "ã‚¿ã‚¹ã‚¯å†…å®¹",

"assignee": "æ‹…å½“è€…", "deadline": "æœŸé™" }} ] }} ], "next_steps": ["æ¬¡å›ã¾ã§

ã®å®¿é¡Œ1", "æ¬¡å›ã¾ã§ã®å®¿é¡Œ2"],

"next_meeting": "æ¬¡å›ä¼šè­°äºˆå®š" }} """ try: response =

self.client.chat.completions.create(

model="gpt-4-turbo-preview", messages=[ {"role": "system", "content": "ã‚

ãªãŸã¯ä¼šè­°ã®è­°äº‹éŒ²ä½œæˆã®å°‚é–€å®¶ã§ã™ã€‚"},

{"role": "user", "content": structuring_prompt} ], temperature=0.3 )

result_text =

response.choices[0].message.content # JSONéƒ¨åˆ†ã‚’æŠ½å‡º json_start =

result_text.find('{') json_end =

result_text.rfind('}') + 1 if json_start != -1 and json_end != -1:

json_text = result_text[json_start:json_end]

structured_minutes = json.loads(json_text) print("âœ… è­°äº‹éŒ²æ§‹é€ åŒ–å®Œäº†")

return structured_minutes else:

print("âŒ JSONå½¢å¼ã®æŠ½å‡ºã«å¤±æ•—") return None except Exception as e:

print(f"âŒ è­°äº‹éŒ²æ§‹é€ åŒ–ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼: {e}") return

None def format_minutes_markdown(self, structured_data: Dict) -> str:

"""æ§‹é€ åŒ–ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ã‚’Markdownå½¢å¼ã«å¤‰æ›""" if

not structured_data: return "" markdown = f"""#

{structured_data.get('meeting_title', 'ä¼šè­°è­°äº‹éŒ²')} **æ—¥æ™‚:**

{structured_data.get('date', datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d'))} **å‚åŠ 

---

## ãƒšãƒ¼ã‚¸ 56

è€…:** {',

'.join(structured_data.get('participants', []))} ## ğŸ“‹ è­°äº‹å†…å®¹ """ for i,

item in

enumerate(structured_data.get('agenda_items', []), 1): markdown += f"""###

{i}. {item.get('topic', '')}

**è­°è«–å†…å®¹:** {item.get('discussion', '')} **æ±ºå®šäº‹é …:** """ for decision in

item.get('decisions', []): markdown

+= f"- {decision}\n" if item.get('action_items'): markdown += "\n**ã‚¢ã‚¯ã‚·ãƒ§

ãƒ³ã‚¢ã‚¤ãƒ†ãƒ :**\n" for action in

item['action_items']: markdown += f"- [ ] {action.get('task', '')} (æ‹…å½“:

{action.get('assignee', 'TBD')}, æœŸé™:

{action.get('deadline', 'TBD')})\n" markdown += "\n---\n\n" if

structured_data.get('next_steps'): markdown +=

"## ğŸ¯ æ¬¡å›ã¾ã§ã®å®¿é¡Œ\n\n" for step in structured_data['next_steps']:

markdown += f"- {step}\n" markdown += "\n"

if structured_data.get('next_meeting'): markdown += f"## ğŸ“… æ¬¡å›ä¼šè­°

\n\n{structured_data['next_meeting']}\n"

return markdown def post_to_slack(self, markdown_content: str, channel:

str = "#general"):

"""Slackã«Markdownè­°äº‹éŒ²ã‚’æŠ•ç¨¿""" if not self.slack_webhook: print("âš  Slack

Webhookæœªè¨­å®š") return #

Markdownã‚’é©åº¦ã«çŸ­ç¸®ã—ã¦Slackç”¨ã«èª¿æ•´ slack_content = markdown_content[:2000]

+ "..." if len(markdown_content) >

2000 else markdown_content payload = { "channel": channel, "username": "è­°

äº‹éŒ²Bot", "text": f"ğŸ“

æ–°ã—ã„è­°äº‹éŒ²ãŒä½œæˆã•ã‚Œã¾ã—ãŸ\n\n```{slack_content}```", "icon_emoji": ":memo:"

} try: response =

requests.post(self.slack_webhook, json=payload) if response.status_code ==

200: print("âœ… SlackæŠ•ç¨¿å®Œäº†") else:

# ãƒ‰ã‚­ãƒ¥ãƒ¡ãƒ³ãƒˆæ¤œç´¢AIã®ç°¡ç•¥ç‰ˆå®Ÿè£… import chromadb from openai import OpenAI

class DocumentSearchAI: def

__init__(self, openai_key: str): self.client = OpenAI(api_key=openai_key)

self.chroma_client = chromadb.Client()

self.collection = self.chroma_client.get_or_create_collection("documents")

def index_documents(self, documents:

List[Dict]): """ãƒ‰ã‚­ãƒ¥ãƒ¡ãƒ³ãƒˆã‚’ãƒ™ã‚¯ãƒˆãƒ«åŒ–ã—ã¦ä¿å­˜""" for doc in documents:

embedding =

self.client.embeddings.create( input=doc['content'], model="text-

embedding-3-small" ).data[0].embedding

self.collection.add( embeddings=[embedding], documents=[doc['content']],

metadatas=[{'title': doc['title'],

'source': doc['source']}], ids=[doc['id']] ) def search_documents(self,

query: str, n_results: int = 3) -> str:

"""è‡ªç„¶è¨€èªã§ãƒ‰ã‚­ãƒ¥ãƒ¡ãƒ³ãƒˆæ¤œç´¢""" # ã‚¯ã‚¨ãƒªã‚’ãƒ™ã‚¯ãƒˆãƒ«åŒ– query_embedding =

self.client.embeddings.create(

input=query, model="text-embedding-3-small" ).data[0].embedding # é¡ä¼¼ãƒ‰ã‚­

ãƒ¥ãƒ¡ãƒ³ãƒˆæ¤œç´¢ results =

self.collection.query( query_embeddings=[query_embedding],

n_results=n_results ) # GPT-4ã§å›ç­”ç”Ÿæˆ context =

"\n".join(results['documents'][0]) answer_prompt = f"è³ªå•:

{query}\n\né–¢é€£æƒ…å ±:\n{context}\n\nä¸Šè¨˜ã®æƒ…å ±ã‚’åŸºã«è³ªå•ã«å›ç­”ã—ã¦ãã ã•ã„ã€‚"

response =

self.client.chat.completions.create( model="gpt-4-turbo-preview",

messages=[{"role": "user", "content":

def calculate_health_scores(self, project_data: Dict) -> Dict: """ãƒ—ãƒ­ã‚¸ã‚§

ã‚¯ãƒˆå¥å…¨æ€§ã‚¹ã‚³ã‚¢è¨ˆç®—""" health_scores

= {} for project in project_data['projects']: # é‡ã¿ä»˜ãç·åˆã‚¹ã‚³ã‚¢ weights =

{ 'productivity': 0.3, 'risk':

-0.25, # ãƒªã‚¹ã‚¯ã¯è² ã®é‡ã¿ 'quality': 0.25, 'communication': 0.2 }

health_score = ( project['productivity'] *

weights['productivity'] + (1 - project['risk']) * abs(weights['risk']) + #

ãƒªã‚¹ã‚¯ã¯é€†è»¢ project['quality'] *

weights['quality'] + project['communication'] * weights['communication'] )

# ã‚¢ãƒ©ãƒ¼ãƒˆãƒ¬ãƒ™ãƒ«åˆ¤å®š if health_score

>= 0.8: alert_level = "ğŸŸ¢ è‰¯å¥½" elif health_score >
